Body language ^MOTaOSYL

Artificially created ^jcKDcKuH

Behavioral component ^u4aWi3Qc

Put yourself in others shoes ^EGLxwPRx

Awareness ^KWEiStbU

What others are doing ^xyGkkGsV

Office = see ^LuyL8V34

IM status ^VCEGB2dJ

Tele presence robots ^s3qWe0rD

Distance = problem ^P3pqxhqp

Shared tools ^b3kOgf9f

Google docs ^UVWRiH4D

Privacy ^boyH6LqF

The feeling of presence is something used to describe the feeling of the
interaction being real, like if it is face to face and the medium is basically 
invisible ^HrCR3ozi

Social presence relates to the feeling of having a human like interaction.
In particular how relatable the other person feel and how warm the conversation
is perceived by the participants.
All this feeling are very influenced by the medium we use to communicate, real time
video and audio communication is the best for this since it allows us to also pick
up on body language and tone, while asynchronous text based communication is 
considered the worst. While it is true that some tools are much better than others
it is also important to consider that how we manage the conversation as a person
can have a huge impact on the warmness of it. If we put in the other person shoes
and pay attention to what we write and how we write we can make the conversation
much better without changing the medium at all  ^tuILSHTo

Awareness is the ability to see what others are
doing and fell like you are with the. The best
scenario for this is of course office work since you
are actually with the team but it is not always
possible. When communicating at distance there are
some ways to increase the awareness, first is a status
feature line in IM systems, that the use of shared
tools like google docs that lets you see in real
time what others are working on, and than some
weirder solutions like tele presence robots, which
are robots with the face of the coworker going
around like if they are there. It is important to
consider that while this systems definitely help
with awareness are a huge problems when we
consider privacy ^TFpY34bB
